#----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#This is a list of words used to "train" Dave Ashley's Wordle strategy program.  The list was
#originally harvested using curl (a standard Utility) from
#
#https://en.m.wiktionary.org/wiki/Wiktionary:Frequency_lists/PG/2006/04/1-10000
#
#and the related web pages that give subsequent members of the list.  The list was then formatted
#from HTML to plain text using various automatic methods (regular expression searching and
#replacing, mostly).
#
#Words containing hyphens, words containing digits, and words containing apostrophes were removed,
#in some cases manually.  It is possible that mistakes were made, and possible that some words
#are missing or duplicated.
#
#Some patently offensive words were removed from the list.
#
#The list of words is in order of decreasing frequency, but there is no absolute frequency
#information contained in the list.
#
#In order to train the  Wordle strategy program, only 5-letter words are considered.
#
#The format of this file is:
#   a)One word per line.
#   b)Words appear in order of decreasing frequency.
#   c)Lines beginning with "#" are comments and are ignored.
#----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
